\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Default AMG coarsening strategy. Coarsening types include:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00122}00122 \textcolor{comment}{    ///  0 = CLJP (parallel coarsening using independent sets)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00123}00123 \textcolor{comment}{    ///  1 = classical RS with no boundary treatment (not recommended}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00124}00124 \textcolor{comment}{    ///      in parallel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00125}00125 \textcolor{comment}{    ///  3 = modified RS with 3rd pass to add C points on the boundaries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00126}00126 \textcolor{comment}{    ///  6 = Falgout (uses 1 then CLJP using interior coarse points as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00127}00127 \textcolor{comment}{    ///      first independent set)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{    ///  8 = PMIS (parallel coarsening using independent sets -\/ lower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{    ///      complexities than 0, maybe also slower convergence)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{    ///  10= HMIS (one pass RS on each processor then PMIS on interior}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{    ///      coarse points as first independent set)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{    ///  11= One pass RS on each processor (not recommended)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{}    \textcolor{comment}{//========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{hypre__solver_8cc_source_l00134}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1HypreHelpers_a8d34acec927aff8f150737afaec9651a}{00134}}     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1HypreHelpers_a8d34acec927aff8f150737afaec9651a}{AMG\_coarsening}} = 6;}
